Wiimote Button Activator [Bully@Wiiplaza]
2865B89A YYYYZZZZ
*YYYY = FFFF - ZZZZ*
*ZZZZ Values*
0004 = Z
0008 = C
0010 = 2
0020 = 1
0040 = -
0080 = +
0100 = B
0200 = A
0400 = D-PAD_RIGHT
0800 = D-PAD_LEFT
1000 = D-PAD_DOWN
2000 = D-PAD_UP
8000 = HOME

Wiimote Button Activator [Bully@Wiiplaza]
28001602 YYYYZZZZ
*Requires "Master Button Activator Wiimote"*
*YYYY = FFFF - ZZZZ
*ZZZZ Values*
0004 = Z
0008 = C
0010 = 2
0020 = 1
0040 = -
0080 = +
0100 = B
0200 = A
0400 = D-PAD_RIGHT
0800 = D-PAD_LEFT
1000 = D-PAD_DOWN
2000 = D-PAD_UP
8000 = HOME
